<h2><span id="English" class="mw-headline">English</span></h2>
<div style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;" class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright">
<div style="float: left;">
<div class="floatnone"><img height="44" width="44" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" alt="" /></div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a title="Wikipedia" href="/wiki/Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:
<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b lang="en" class="Latn"><a title="w:Wiktionary" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wiktionary">Wiktionary</a></b></div>

<span class="interProject"></span></div>
<h3><span id="Etymology" class="mw-headline">Etymology</span></h3>
<p><a title="Appendix:Glossary" href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#blend">Blend</a> of <i lang="en" class="Latn mention"><a title="wiki" href="/wiki/wiki#English">wiki</a></i> + <i lang="en" class="Latn mention"><a title="dictionary" href="/wiki/dictionary#English">dictionary</a></i>.</p>

<h3><span id="Proper_noun" class="mw-headline">Proper noun</span></h3>
<p><strong lang="en" class="Latn headword">Wiktionary</strong> (<i>plural</i> <span class="form-of lang-en proper-noun-plural-form-of"><b lang="en" class="Latn"><a title="Wiktionaries" href="/wiki/Wiktionaries#English">Wiktionaries</a></b></span>)</p>
<ol>
<li>A <a title="collaborative" href="/wiki/collaborative">collaborative</a> project run by the <a title="w:Wikimedia Foundation" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a> to produce a <a title="free" href="/wiki/free">free</a> and <a title="complete" href="/wiki/complete">complete</a> <a title="dictionary" href="/wiki/dictionary">dictionary</a> in every <a title="language" href="/wiki/language">language</a>.</li>
<li>The dictionaries, collectively, produced by that project.</li>
<li>A particular version of this dictionary project, written in a certain language, such as the English-language Wiktionary or simply the English Wiktionary.</li>
</ol>
<h4><span id="Quotations" class="mw-headline">Quotations</span></h4>
<p><span class="see-cites">For usage examples of this term, see <a title="Citations:Wiktionary" href="/wiki/Citations:Wiktionary#English">Citations:Wiktionary</a>.</span></p>

<h3><span id="Etymology_2" class="mw-headline">Etymology</span></h3>

<h3><span id="Etymology_3" class="mw-headline">Etymology</span></h3>
<p><a title="Appendix:Glossary" href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#loanword">Borrowing</a> from <span class="etyl"><a title="w:English language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language">English</a></span> <i lang="en" class="Latn mention"><a title="Wiktionary" href="/wiki/Wiktionary#English">Wiktionary</a></i>.</p>
